Consult with Chen Tiaoyuan on Defense Matters

Jinan Correspondence: Ma Hongkui arrived in Jining on the evening of the 22nd. He had originally planned to come to Jinan earlier to discuss defense matters with Chen Tiaoyuan, but due to the need to properly arrange the defenses of his troops, he did not arrive until 12:00 noon today, traveling north by special train from Jining. Gu Zhutong also needed to discuss defense matters in southern Shandong with Chen Tiaoyuan, so he traveled north with Ma on the same train. They departed from Yanzhou at 1:30 PM and arrived in Tai'an at 4:30 PM. The headquarters here arranged rooms for Ma and Gu at the Shitaiyan Hotel on Shangbu Dama Road and ordered the First Garrison Brigade to dispatch a company of soldiers, along with the provincial government military band, to welcome them at the station. Important News Two

Martial Law Implemented in Bengbu 74

Bengbu Correspondence: The local security here was previously under the responsibility of the 11th Division, as ordered by Liu Zhi, the commander-in-chief of the Second Route Army. Recently, Commander-in-Chief Chiang (Kai-shek) stated that the situation in Bengbu was extremely important in the rear area, and that martial law should be implemented during this military period. He appointed Chen Cheng, the commander of the 11th Division, as the martial law commander of Bengbu. After receiving the order, Chen came to Bengbu to organize the martial law headquarters, establishing three sections: staff, adjutant, and military law. The section chiefs of the staff, adjutant, and military law sections of the 11th Division concurrently served as the heads of the corresponding sections in the headquarters. The headquarters was located in the 11th Division headquarters in the Huadong Apartment. The joint military-police inspection office was merged into the martial law headquarters, and Huo Kuizhang, the commander of the 64th Regiment of the 32nd Brigade under Chen Cheng's command, was appointed as the chief of the inspection office. The inspection office was still jointly organized by the military and police and was located in the General Chamber of Commerce. A patrol team was also established, dividing the city into three districts and assigning patrols to each district. Military and police officers from the inspection office inspected travelers arriving and departing from the train station, riverboat wharf, and bus station every day. Chen Cheng assumed the position of martial law commander on the 25th and issued the following announcement: "I have received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek, which reads: 'Chen Cheng, the commander of the 11th Division, is hereby appointed as the martial law commander of Bengbu. Martial law is to be implemented immediately, and the local government is to be consulted on conducting a census and obtaining joint guarantees. The appointment certificate and seal will be issued separately. You are to comply diligently and report accordingly.' I have received the telegram and assumed office today, commencing martial law. In addition to reporting and distributing this announcement, this announcement is hereby issued for general awareness." (March 25th)

Zhang Guangwu, Assassin of Wu Luzhen 75

Sentenced to Ten Years in Prison by the Shandong High Court

Jinan Correspondence: Wu Luzhen, a pioneer of the revolution, was assassinated by Zhang Guangwu, the battalion commander of the guard company under Yuan Shikai's command, in the year of the Xinhai Revolution. It was not until the success of the revolution, in the 18th year, when the Shandong Provincial Government was in Tai'an, that Zhang was arrested after being reported. After repeated trials by the Shandong High Court, Judge Ouyang Xu, Liu Dexun, and Wang Mianshan announced the verdict in court yesterday. Zhang Guangwu was sentenced to ten years of imprisonment for anti-revolutionary conspiracy to commit murder, and deprived of his civil rights for fifteen years. The judgment is recorded as follows:

"The defendant, Zhang Guangwu, is sentenced as follows after being tried by this court for the crime of anti-revolution:

Principal Sentence: Zhang Guangwu is sentenced to ten years of imprisonment, deprived of his civil rights for fifteen years, for organizing a group and carrying out important tasks with the aim of anti-revolution, and jointly committing murder. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined will be counted as one day of imprisonment for every two days.

Reasons: The case will be explained in three parts below. (1) Evidence of the crime: The defendant has stated that he served in the First Jingji Zhen in Beijing, directly under the Ministry of the Army, first under the control of Tie Liang, and then under the command of Yin Chang. He also rotated to garrison the Beiyuan and guard the Forbidden City and the Imperial Tombs. It can be seen that he was a trusted confidant of the Qing imperial family. Furthermore, the informant, Liu Hanmin, repeatedly testified that he boasted in his hometown about participating in the assassination of Wu. Moreover, the county citizens Men Ti Yun, Liu Yinbin, Wang Jianxun, Huang Yannian, and Xu Yunzhong submitted consistent statements. The county magistrate replied in his report that after extensive investigation, it was confirmed that when Wu Luzhen was assassinated, the defendant returned home from outside and boasted to the public, which was known to all. The judges and prosecutors of the county court reported that the defendant did boast about assassinating Wu in his hometown, and they obtained statements from Zhang Qinsheng and Zhang Ling, who lived in the same village as the defendant, confirming that the defendant boasted about assassinating Wu. The Provincial Party Department 指委會 and the County Party Department 指委會 also stated that the defendant was the main perpetrator of the assassination of Wu, and that many reports at the time had been published. (See the provincial government files.) If there was no such thing, why would all the legal authorities and the majority of the people agree on the same thing? Moreover, the defendant stated that he had no grudges against the informant, Liu Hanmin. In addition, the era of the martyr's assassination was long ago, and the events were extraordinary, so there would be no baseless accusations. Based on this observation, it is sufficient to conclude that the defendant participated in the assassination of Wu. (2) The defendant's defense: There are two pieces of evidence that the defendant claims are proof against the charges. (1) He submitted documents such as awards, certificates, and commissions from various official positions, stating that he had served in the First Division from the 31st year of Guangxu to the 2nd year of the Republic of China for eight or nine years. In the 3rd year of Xuantong, he suffered from numbness in his hands due to the wind in the Western Mausoleums and asked for leave to return home. He was not a guard battalion commander under Yuan Shikai, so how could he have been instigated by Yuan to assassinate Wu? (To be continued)

Renewed Fighting in Guangxi Province 76

Contact in the Areas of Pingnan, Jiangkou, Guixian, and Xingye for Days

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangxi war situation, which had been in a ceasefire for a long time, has recently returned to a state of gunpowder smoke. The Zhang-Gui army has since

Tang Shengming's troops,

Their arrangement is that Zhang's army will attack Gaozhou again from Qinzhou and Lianzhou in Guangdong, which is the right wing. The Gui army will attack Wuzhou along the Dahe River from Pingnan, taking charge of the central route. Bai Chongxi and Tang Shengming's troops will leave Fuxing and head to Hexian, attempting to copy Guangning and Huaiji, which is the left route. Recently, the military strength of the Sixth and Eighth Route Armies has also been replenished, and the vacancies have been filled. They took the opportunity to clear out the Zhang-Gui army to prevent the war from prolonging and plunging the people into misery. Therefore, the general offensive order was issued on the evening of the 16th. Zhang Fakui's army Anpu Gaozhou, there are only the Zhang Zhiying Regiment and Xu Zhen Ying of the Eighth Route Army, who fought fiercely with the enemy for three days and nights.

Chen Zhangfu, the commander of the Southern Route Garrison Command, departed by ship and landed in Shuidong, which belongs to Gaozhou, intending to recruit the old troops of the two first, and then advance to Gaozhou. At the same time, the Eighth Route Army on the Guangxi border had to launch a fierce attack on Xingye on the border between Guangxi and Guangdong due to the activities of Zhang's army on the Southern Route, so that Zhang's army would not dare to Gao Lei.

Jiang Guangnai's division commanded the Li Deying and Gong Shouyi regiments of Lv Huanyan in Yulin, and launched a fierce attack on Xingye. On the 16th, Li Deying's regiment was 20 miles above Yulin and contacted the Huang Shaoxiong troops of the Gui army. He has now crossed Huaiping, which is the most recent progress of the left wing of the Eighth Route Army. As for the central route, the Yu Hanmou Division of the Eighth Route Army and the Guo Siyan artillery regiment of Jiang's division have gathered in Tengxian. Zhou Xinming's newly编师部 is stationed above Tengxian. Recently, due to the heavy rain in Guangxi Province, the river channels have risen. The Eighth Route Army has chartered more than 200民船 from Guangzhou to Wuzhou to attack along the Dahe River. The Sixth Route Army is also advancing from Fengchuan to the Wuxu Rongwei in Wuzhou. Zhu Shaoliang moved the headquarters of the Sixth Route Army to Wuzhou. Tao's brigade of his troops has already stationed a part of its troops in Tengxian, and Mao's division is guarding Majiang. According to reliable information, the two armies have been in contact in Pingnan and Jiangkou along the Fuxing River. On the 19th, He Peiji, the staff officer of the Sixth Route Army 行营, sent a telegram detailing the recent military situation in the front. The telegram is recorded as follows: "To Yang Cice, the military law officer of the Sixth Route Army Headquarters 駐省辦事處 on Panfu Road, Guangzhou. I have received a report from Zhou Xinming, the commander of the Xunliu Garrison Command of Guangxi, as ordered by the commander-in-chief. The main points are as follows: (1) The newly编第一团 of his unit (i.e., Zhou's unit),团长刘耀章, gathered his troops in Siwangwei, Pingnan County on the 15th night and immediately occupied Pingnan. After several hours of mixed fighting, the enemy army came to support with a regiment from Guiping in the morning, and our army engaged in fierce fighting. (2) The troops of Second Regiment Commander Lv Dingxiang simultaneously launched an attack, leading a team of about five or six hundred people from Bitan and occupied Daheng Jiangkouwei nearby. (3) The enemy army 李世奇 Regiment, which was reorganized by his unit, sent people to ask for help in Dawa, requesting that the front army be ordered to advance and rescue quickly. (4) The deputy officer Chen Qicai led the First Independent Battalion in Daguishan near Pingnan, and one battalion of the First Regiment, and Lv Dingxiang's troops of the Second Regiment, waiting for orders to advance and respond to the planned advance on Pingnan, and join in attacking Guiping. (5) There are about three regiments of enemy troops along the Dahe River from Guiping to Guixian, occupying different areas. Among them, the He Cisanyi and Wang Zanbin regiments have sent representatives to contact and prepare to surrender, and are responsible for internal response. They have received appointment orders, and it is hoped that our army will逼攻潯, so that it will be easy to solve. (6) Yang Tenghui's and Bai Chongxi's troops guard Shixing 石龍 in Wuxuan to Liuzhou. Li Zongren, Huang Shaoxiong, and Zhang Fakui's troops are concentrated in Binyang and Nanning. (7) The headquarters (i.e., the headquarters of the Sixth Route Army) will move to Rongxu on the 20th. (8) The various armies under this route began to advance towards Mengjiang on the 17th. Hao Chenyin, the staff office of the Sixth Route Army's Wuzhou 行营. (March 21st)

Good Governance on the Beining Railway 77

Accepting the Opinions of the Business Conference

Shanhaiguan Abolishes Military Surtax

Tianjin Correspondence: The Beining Railway Bureau convened a business conference earlier.

At that time, merchants along the railway line, both inside and outside the pass, unanimously requested Shanhaiguan to change and

correct its tax collection procedures and abolish the military surtax. At that time,

representatives of various chambers of commerce presented four requests to the customs: (1) Simplify the

inspection procedures for goods transported by rail when passing through the customs at the pass. (2) For package goods transported by rail,

some may not be able to declare taxes in time due to the absence of merchant escorts. Please

extend the deadline for penalties. (3) Please reduce the customs duties on direct transport of goods between Yingkou and Tongliao, and between Yingkou and Shenyang. (4) Please exempt the

20% military surtax collected by the Regular Customs. The above four

items were publicly declared by the customs representative, Section Chief Gu Jinsheng,

that the representatives of the Customs Superintendent's Office would accommodate and consider them. After the meeting, the

Office immediately sent a letter to the Beining Railway stating that for commercial goods,

taxes should be strictly inspected and paid at the place of departure. All places passed through, except the

Shanhaiguan, Goubangzi, Jin County, and Yixian bureaus, are generally exempt from

inspection to facilitate commercial transportation. As for the second item regarding the transportation of parcels, the

tax collection period is approved to be extended to seven days. Penalties will only be imposed after seven days. Also, for the third item, goods transported by road between Yingkou and Tongliao, and between Yingkou and Shenyang,

the current tax of one yuan per ton

will be reduced to sixty cents. Yesterday, the Beining Railway Bureau also approved a letter from the Customs

Superintendent's Office stating that regarding the fourth

item requested by the chamber of commerce representatives, to exempt the 20% military surtax from the Regular Customs,

it has also been submitted to the Liaoning Provincial Government for approval and will be exempted from April 1 this

year. The losses incurred after the exemption will be addressed by formulating other methods and adjusting

subsidies from the Railway Bureau. The four items requested by the Chamber of Commerce have now been completely and satisfactorily resolved

.

Furthermore, the Tianzhuangtai Station on the Yingkou branch line of the Beining Railway is rich in products.

In order to compete for transportation, the Railway Bureau reduced the original price of nine

yuan and seven

yuan per ton for the transportation of third, fourth, and fifth class goods between that station and Shenyang last year to three yuan. However, due to the heavy taxes from the Regular Customs,

freight transport did not improve. Also, freight transport between Yingkou and Xinmin has always been

brisk, but for the transportation of general goods by rail, about every twenty tons required

paying more than three hundred yuan in taxes. In order to avoid heavy taxes, merchants

mostly switched to transportation via the Liao River waterway. Therefore, although the Railway Bureau repeatedly reduced freight

rates, it was still unable to reverse the downward trend. Now, the Bureau has sent personnel to investigate

and has obtained the truth. The investigators also went to Yingkou to meet with the

Shanhaiguan Superintendent Hong to discuss relief measures. According to the report of the investigators,

they have obtained Superintendent Hong's permission, but the extent of the reduction

will have to wait for the railway and chamber of commerce to conduct thorough research before it can be submitted to the Liaoning Provincial Government for approval and implementation, so as to

prevent the products of Northeast China from being exported through ports operated by foreigners in order to avoid heavy taxes. The original letter from the Shanhaiguan Superintendent's Office regarding the cessation of the

20% Surtax for Post-Disaster Relief Expenses is recorded below: "According to an investigation of a business conference convened by your bureau in

December of last year, merchants appealed for the exemption of the 20% surtax for post-disaster relief expenses from the Regular Customs in order to alleviate the burden. The

Superintendent submitted a special report to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee for approval and

forwarded a copy of the draft letter for your reference. Now, an order has been received stating that the

Superintendent's report on the Beining Railway Business Conference resolution to exempt the

20% surtax for post-disaster relief expenses has been ordered by the Committee to be sent to the Liaoning

Provincial Government for careful deliberation and prompt reply for approval.

Now, according to the report from Zang Shiyi, Chairman of the Liaoning Provincial Government, an

instruction No. 13 from your Committee has been received stating that according to the report from the Shanhaiguan Superintendent

regarding the Beining Railway Business Conference resolution to exempt the additional 20%

surtax for post-disaster relief expenses, a copy of the review outline should be attached to determine whether this surtax should be approved for exemption.

The Liaoning Provincial Government is ordered to deliberate carefully and reply promptly for approval. This order includes two attached copies, etc.

Therefore, the matter was brought up for discussion at the 95th Provincial Committee meeting. It was unanimously agreed that exempting this surtax

is for the purpose of alleviating the hardship of merchants and facilitating transportation and should be followed. However, there is no guarantee that

tax revenues will be prosperous in the future. If there are losses as a result, other methods of compensation should be considered.

If the Beining Railway can provide appropriate subsidies at that time, difficulties can be avoided. It was decided that the surtax

would be exempted, and the road subsidy method in the future would be submitted together for transfer to the

said railway for notification. The circumstances are hereby reported for your Committee's consideration and

separate instructions for implementation. After investigation, since this case has been decided by the Provincial Committee to be exempted,

and the road subsidy method in the future should be approved as

reported. In addition to instructions and separate orders, an order is hereby issued for immediate

compliance. Based on this, an investigation has been made and the 20% surtax for post-disaster relief expenses from the Regular Customs has been

approved for exemption. It should be implemented from April 1 this

year. In addition to reporting and issuing notices to all bureaus and posting a notice for all merchants to comply with,

a corresponding letter is hereby sent for your reference. To the Beining Railway

Administration."

Local Correspondence

Kunshan 78

Eleven Kidnapped Residents of Zhangpu Town Released: Zhangpu Town was recently raided by lake bandits,

and 57 men, women, and children were kidnapped. It is now known that on the 26th,

Tong Meisheng, Zeng Tangshi, Zhu Shouyi, and eleven others were released by the bandits' boats.

Yesterday, they came to Kunshan by car from Suzhou. According to Tong and others, on that day (the

23rd), they were driven onto the boats by the bandits and transported to a certain place to disembark. In an open space,

the bandit leader, about 30 years old, questioned the hostages one by one

before returning them to the boats. There were a total of 18 bandit boats, with ample firearms and

more than 200 people. In addition to the people from Zhangpu, there were also two people from Jiaxing

on the boats. Zhang Bochen, a kidnapped resident of Zhangpu, was shot dead by the bandits and thrown

into the river for disobeying their orders. At about 1:00 AM on the 26th, the bandits arrived near Yangcheng

Lake and ordered Tong and others to disembark and guard until dawn. They met local villagers (the

location was between Chefang and Gaodian) and, after recounting the kidnapping, the villagers there

collected 20 silver dollars and pointed out the way to Suzhou before taking a car to

Kunshan. It is said that the lake bandits were once members of the local defense force in the town last year

and guest residents.

Lake Bandits Near Ba City Again Rob a Small Steamboat: In Zhaojiawan, about three miles away from Ba City Town,

more than 20 bandit boats arrived at 4:00 PM on the 25th, with two to three hundred lake bandits, fully equipped with firearms. The villagers, seeing this,

immediately reported to the Public Security Sub-Bureau and the District Office. After receiving the report, Sub-Bureau Chief Wang Zhengben and District Chief

Wang Wuqing immediately joined forces with the county police team and defense force patrols stationed there to

strictly guard the main roads and fire warning shots.

Before long, the bandits came, but seeing the precautions, they immediately retreated to their original position.

At around 7:00 PM, the Yongji steamboat of the Tongli Company, which runs between Shanghai and Changshu,

towing two company boats, passed through the area and was stopped from proceeding by the bandits.

The bandits immediately jumped onto the steamboat and first moved 30 pieces of factory cloth

on the steamboat to the bandit boats. Then, they searched the passengers' luggage and money,

including four leather suitcases belonging to someone from Changshu who was transporting them to Shanghai, which were also robbed.

Fortunately, no one was injured. After an hour, they crossed the boat and sailed into Yangcheng Lake

before leaving. After seeing the bandits leave, the steamboat sailed to Ba City and reported to the County Government on the morning of the 26th, requesting an investigation.

A Large Number of Gamblers Arrested: On the afternoon of the 26th, Zhou Wusan, Chief of the Kunshan County Public Security Bureau,

learned that a large number of gamblers were gathering at the Weng residence in Fengchebang in the city. He immediately ordered Inspector Lv Tan to lead a

platoon of police officers to rush to the scene and make arrests. Twenty-four

gamblers, including Xu A'kui, were caught on the spot, along with gambling tools. They were taken to the bureau for interrogation. The gamblers all confessed to gambling

without denying it and were immediately fined separately.

Temple are estimated to require 5,000 yuan. In addition to convening district chiefs to raise funds, there is still a shortage of 2,000 yuan. In addition to various organizations

holding meetings on their own to discuss raising funds, the County Government specially convened the county

bar association today to discuss funding issues. It is heard that the lawyers are

making unremitting efforts to promote the early establishment of the county court. Therefore, in addition to the original subscription,

they have agreed to continue to subscribe 500 yuan. The approximate amount of the shortfall will have to be borne by

various organizations.

Daughter-in-law Sues Uncle for Rape: Yu Xiaodi, a resident of He Ye Dai in the city, has no

heirs and plans to adopt his cousin A'chang, who lives with him. However, A'chang and his wife often

spoke disrespectfully to Xiaodi and repeatedly quarreled. Yu Xiaodi reported this to the Second District Sub-Station, and

A'chang and his wife were summoned for questioning. It was originally intended to slightly reprimand them so that they could return to harmony. However, the cousin's wife resented the uncle's report

and falsely accused Xiaodi of attempting to rape her without success and falsely reported the arrest, etc.

According to the confession, Field Inspector Tian prepared a document and sent it to the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Yu A'chang was sentenced to 15 days of detention for disobeying his uncle. The cousin's wife's false accusation of rape was extremely shameless and she was released in court.

Suzhou 81

Thirty-Six Families Robbed in Hanzhen Township: On the afternoon of the 23rd,

more than 100 bandits came to Hanzhen Township in Zhouzhuang County and robbed 36 families,

losing 364 yuan and 88 dou and 5 sheng of white rice. Yesterday, the victims reported to the county for investigation.

Calls for Rising Rice Prices: The price of rice in Suzhou City has risen

from 14 yuan to 15 yuan per shi. In the past week, it has suddenly risen by another yuan. Poor

common people will have no way to seek a full meal. Seeing this situation, it is feared that it will affect local public order. The Suzhou Rice Industry Workers' Union

specially convened an emergency meeting on the afternoon of the 26th and resolved: (1) Request the Yicang

Management Committee to purchase the cheapest foreign rice in Shanghai and open a store to sell it at a fair price. (2) Telegraph various party and government agencies to consider the livelihood of the poor and notify the

union to implement the opening of fair-price rice sales immediately to alleviate the suffering of the people of Suzhou. It is heard that there are still unscrupulous merchants coming to Suzhou to transport rice abroad. In the past week,

more than 30,000 shi have been purchased and transported out of the country in various rural areas. The future of the people's food is

unthinkable.

Lake Bandits Rampant in Yangcheng Lake: A large gang of lake bandits, about 400 to 500 people, recently arrived in the Yangcheng Lake area of the county,

traveling in more than 40 boats. The Taihu Bandit Suppression Command has received intelligence and ordered Gong, the district chief of the Third Water Public Security District,

and the bandit suppression troops to rush to suppress them.

Li-Cheng Mutual Accusation Case Continues Hearing: The case of former Prime Minister Li Genyuan and

his concubine Cheng Peiyi mutually accusing each other has been repeatedly heard by the Wu County District Court.

Li has entrusted lawyer Tang Shenfang to appear in court on his behalf. The court ordered both parties to settle out of court, but Cheng Peiyi refused

and applied for a summons for Li to appear in court in person. The court is scheduled to continue

the hearing this afternoon (the 28th).

Wuxi 82

Thugs Murdered Beat Policeman: Wei Jinshan, a beat policeman from the Tenth Post of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau outside the South Gate of the county,

was on duty at around 9:00 PM the night before when he saw the young owner of a meat shop in Huangniqiao whispering with a Jiangbei

person. Before long, the Jiangbei person suddenly reported to the beat policeman Wei Jinshan that someone was fighting in a workshop on the south side and asked him to quickly

mediate. Policeman Wei believed it to be true and followed him. Unexpectedly,

when he arrived at the Huangbaoche Shop at the junction of Yangming Township, two people suddenly

came forward and grabbed the policeman. The Jiangbei person who was traveling with him also immediately

seized a pistol that Wei was carrying and tied him up with a rope.

He pushed Wei into the river there, hoping to kill him. Fortunately, the rope was not tied tightly, and Wei

struggled to break free and swam ashore. He went to a nearby tailor shop,

took off his wet clothes, and asked the tailor shop owner Shen Erda to report to the

bureau. Upon receiving the report, Branch Chief Zhu immediately sent police officers to

bring Wei back. After questioning him, he sent Patrol Chief Gu Liewu and Xun Gongting to bring Wei

to arrest Liu A'si and Guan Chengfu, Liu Yuzhang, and others.

Xu Yunzhang, the young owner of the meat shop, was summoned to the bureau and sent to the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation. The

more than 20 shops on Nanxin Road jointly submitted a report to the Public Security Bureau,

accusing the Third Branch of retaliating, falsely reporting a drowning,

harming good citizens, and requesting that the policeman Wei Jinshan be thoroughly investigated for falsely reporting the situation. After the case was transferred to the bureau, Zhang, a staff member, opened the court at 5:00 PM to investigate.

Wei Jinshan confessed to the previous situation. When asked, Liu A'si and the other four

did not admit it. Wei was ordered to return home, and Liu and the other four were released on bail pending

investigation and handling.

Taihu Bandit Suppression Army Prepares for Mobilization: Hu Zuyu, the commander-in-chief of the Taihu Bandit Suppression Army,

believes that the bandit suppression troops have already been deployed properly and will mobilize to suppress the bandits soon.

The telephone lines, boats, and other equipment needed must be prepared as soon as possible.

Yesterday, he issued separate orders to the commanders of the east and west regions, Zhao Xiguang and Zhong Yuan,

and the county governments to immediately contact and negotiate the completion of Article 4 of the bandit suppression plan

so that they could mobilize as soon as possible.

Robbery and Murder Case: The Yongren Cocoon Shop in Heshang Bridge, Qingcheng City, in the county, was

robbed last year, resulting in a significant loss. Unexpectedly, on the evening of January 17 this

year, more than 10 bandits suddenly came to Wu Lane in the city and robbed the families of Wu Yuemao, Wu Qiuquan, and Wu Longbo.

Wu Shisheng, Wu Yuemao's father, and Wu Xue, his mother, were injured with sticks. Wu Qiuquan

was also burned by the bandits. After the incident, the county police team arrested Wang Baofu (i.e., Wang Baopu),

a bandit involved in the case, and interrogated him. Wang

confessed to robbing the Yongren Cocoon Shop and the families of Wu Yuemao and the other three.

County Chief Sun prepared a document recording the confession and submitted it to the provincial government for approval. Yesterday (

the 27th), at 10:00 AM, police officers bound the bandit Wang Baofu and took him

to the large training ground next to the railway station for execution by firing squad to serve as a warning.

Li Chengguo, a fugitive wanted for escaping from the detention center, was also a principal offender in the robbery of the families of Wu Yuemao and the other three in Wu Lane.

It is deeply regrettable that he escaped this time.

East Guanshe Village Reported Robbery Alert: Yu Xiangzhou, a resident of East Guanshe Village, at the junction of Kaiyuan and Yangming Townships in the county,

runs an iron shop in Zhenjiang and is considered well-to-do. At around 11:00 PM the night before, five

bandits came to Yu's residence,

holding a fake pistol and using cars and bamboo poles as weapons. They entered the room from outside and

held Yu's wife and daughter together, overturning boxes

and opening baskets to search and rob at will. After about an hour, they carried the stolen goods away.

Afterwards, it was discovered that clothing, jewelry, silver dollars, etc. had been robbed, resulting in a loss of about three

thousand yuan.

The County Government Offers Rewards for the Arrest of Fugitives: On the night before, at around 2:00 AM,

Li Chengguo, Zhang A'qi, Wang A'san, Wu Xirong, Yuan A'san, Zhang A'quan, Liu Erxiazi, and seven

other fugitives escaped from two new cells in the county government's detention center. It is now known that yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, Zhou, a reviewer from the County Government,

opened the court to interrogate Dai A'bing, Cai Heyuan, Yu A'jiu, and fifteen

other inmates who had not escaped from the same cell, as well as Liu Yinqiu, the secretary of the branch, and Jiang Hai and Lin, the guards on duty.

All confessed that they were unaware of the situation. Secretary Liu and the guards Jiang Hai and Lin stated that

they had not known in advance and that there was no bribery involved. After the interrogation, the inmates were returned

to custody, and Liu and Jiang were placed under guard by the duty police pending verification. At the same time,

County Chief Sun issued a proclamation

offering rewards for the arrest of the fugitives. A reward of

200 silver dollars will be given to military personnel or civilians who capture Li Chengguo, and a reward of

100 silver dollars will be given to those who capture Zhang A'qi, Wang A'san, Wu Xirong, Yuan A'san,

Zhang A'quan, and Liu Erxiazi.

Changzhou 83

Tangjiaba Robbery and Murder Case: Near Tangjiaba in Jiaoxi Town, Wu County,

Shi Xingda's family was attacked. At around 1:00 AM on the 26th, more than

10 bandits suddenly came with pistols and flashlights and broke into the house. After going upstairs, they first shot Shi's wife, Ms. Liu, in the throat, and she immediately fell to the

ground and died. Shi Xingda was also beaten and injured. All silver dollars, clothing, and jewelry were robbed.

After the incident, it was reported to the county by the Fifth District Office for verification by a commissioner.

Police Team Arrests Kidnappers: Gao Lianhai, a bandit from Xiaoliuqiao, Weicun Town, Wu County,

kidnapped a young child surnamed Yang and received a ransom of several thousand yuan.

He divided the spoils at home. Recently, he extorted silver dollars from Gao Jizhang. Gao reported this to the police team stationed in the town, and they were arrested.

He confessed to having received a share of the ransom money and extorted silver dollars. He was sent to the County Court for interrogation on the 26th.

County Magistrate Reassigns Two District Chiefs: Cheng Foyu, District Chief of the Tenth District of Wu County,

resigned due to illness. On the 26th, County Chief Zhu approved the reassignment of Zhao Yi, the District Chief of the Seventh District, to fill the position.

The vacancy of District Chief of the Seventh District was filled by Yue Jun.

At the same time, Zhu Shoukang was appointed as Assistant of the Sixth District, and Zhai Hao as Assistant of the Seventh District.

Land Reclamation Case Re-Emerges: The land reclamation rent increase dispute in Yiling City in the eastern part of the county

District Office Funding Problems: The funding for various district offices in Nantong is seriously

8 li per mu. Now, the Finance Department has ordered that it should be reported to determine whether the collection of the donation has

exceeded 1% of the land price.

Bandits Attempt to Attack Luzhuang: On the morning of the 23rd,

more than 2,000 bandits suddenly attacked Lujiazhuang in the Lugang District of Rugao, carrying more than 100 guns

and many earth cannons, in two routes. Chen Qingxun, the commander of the second squadron of the garrisoned county police team, ordered the security force of the village to meet them in the west

northwest, and personally led more than 10 county police to suppress them in the southwest. At the same time,

a special person was sent to Xiabao to mobilize and gather a large force to assist in the suppression. After a fierce battle until 7:00

AM, the bandits were unable to hold out and fled. At that time, the provincial police teams stationed in Huangqiao and Guxi heard the news and rushed to assist in the pursuit and suppression. In this battle, more than 50 bandits were killed

, 11 were captured alive, and one earth cannon was seized. The heads of three killed bandits were cut off and sent back to the county town for public display. When suppressing the bandits,

Lu Zixun, the current assistant of the district office in Luzhuang, and Lu

five houses, were burned down.

Jiashan 87

Detailed Account of the Robbery of the Qingping Commercial Steamboat: On the morning of the 25th, the

Qingyuan commercial steamboat of Wang Qingji in Shanyi, which sails between Luxu and Wang Qingji, was sailing to Qianjing Port, a place about three

miles away from Xitang in Fanjing, when two bandit boats suddenly came.

Six or seven bandits, wearing gray military uniforms and holding guns, fired

several shots and ordered the ship to stop. Dozens of passengers on the ship were

not spared. Wang Angru, a partner of Yongfu Village, was on the steamboat being towed,

carrying a total of 5,000 yuan in 10-yuan and 5-yuan banknotes from the China Communications Bank, as well as a wool-blend mandarin jacket and more than 40 yuan in banknotes in his pocket, all of which were

robbed. In addition, 50,000 yuan in banknotes from the Bank of China, which were stuffed in the bottom of the cabin, were

not robbed. The previous rumors of the robbery were mistaken. In addition, Yang Baobao, the fiancee of Cao Qilin, the head of the Xitang Branch Bureau, had clothing and other items

robbed, worth more than 200 yuan. When the incident occurred, Chen Shilong, the captain of the Eighth

Water Police Team stationed in Xitang, happened to be attending a district meeting in Jiaxing and did not dispatch the team to pursue

the bandits. The urban area was under special martial law that night for defense. Currently, the people of Xitang

are in a state of panic because there are rumors that the bandits will rob Xitang. Therefore, the responsible agencies are

intensifying the defense of the town day and night.

Hangzhou 88

Ningbo 89

Chairman Chiang Visits Yulin'ao to Sweep Graves: Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the National Government, taking advantage of this inspection, returned to his hometown to sweep graves. Yesterday (the 25th) at 9 a.m., he prepared sacrificial offerings and, accompanied by his wife, Soong Mei-ling, departed from Wenchang Pavilion in Xikou, traveling by carriage to Baiyan Mountain Temple in Yulin'ao to sweep the grave of his late mother. Chiang Chieh-ching (Chairman's elder brother) and more than a dozen male and female relatives also went, one after another. More than two hundred students from Wuling Elementary School also went in formation to participate. After setting up the altar in front of the grave, Chairman Chiang first performed the kowtow ceremony, followed by Madame Soong Mei-ling, who bowed three times. Then, his elder brother Chiang Chieh-ching and relatives offered their respects. Representatives from Wuling Elementary School presented wreaths and sang a grave-sweeping song. On the same day, Zhang Jingjiang, Zhu Jiahua, Chen Bulei, and others visited Xuebao Temple. Upon hearing that Chairman Chiang was sweeping graves in Yulin'ao, they immediately rushed to participate in the sacrificial ceremony. Shortly after, they returned to Xuebao Temple to visit. Chairman Chiang, after completing the grave sweeping, rested at the tomb estate and had lunch with relatives. He returned to his residence in Xikou at about 3 p.m. Zhang Jingjiang, Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, and Zhu Jiahua, Chen Bulei, Shen Shiyuan, and others from the Provincial Committee, returned to Wuling Elementary School in Xikou at about 3 p.m. At 7 p.m., they bid farewell to Chairman Chiang and, accompanied by Zhou Junyan, the Salt Transport Commissioner of Liangzhe, departed in three cars to Ningbo. This morning at 8 a.m., they took the express train back to Hangzhou.

Chen Shaokuan Leaves Fengtian to Return to Nanjing: Chen Shaokuan, Acting Minister of the Navy, accompanied Chairman Chiang to Fengtian the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, he received an order from the Chairman to return to Nanjing first and ordered the Chu Tai warship to return to Shanghai. The Jiankang warship, which escorted them to Ningbo, was ordered to remain in Ningbo. After receiving the order, Minister Chen left Fengtian for Ningbo at 9 a.m. yesterday. Today, he will take the Chu Tai warship to Shanghai and then to Nanjing to handle affairs and report to the Central Committee members on the situation in Fengtian on behalf of Chairman Chiang.

Letter Received

Letter from the Jiaxing Branch of the Bank of China 90

To the Editor,

With regards to the news item published in the "Domestic Important Telegrams" column of your newspaper on March 26 concerning the Qingping small steamer being robbed in Fan Jing, which stated that the manager of the Jiaxing branch of the Bank of China was robbed of 50,000 yuan in cash, this is not the case. It is a misunderstanding based on hearsay. We hereby issue a statement and request that you publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" column to correct the record.

Sincerely,

Jiaxing Branch of the Bank of China

Shandong Province Sends 13 Athletes 101

Iron Ball Athlete Zhang Ziyuan Unable to Attend

Shandong Department of Education Sends Off Athletes with 40 Yuan in Travel Expenses

Jinan Quick News, 24th - The Shandong preliminary competition for the National Games was held at the Jinan Public Sports Field on the 23rd. It was originally decided to send 14 athletes to Hangzhou to participate in the National Games. However, due to an issue, Zhang Ziyuan (iron ball athlete), the accountant at the Taian Railway Station ticket office, could not go. Therefore, it was changed to sending 13 people: two javelin throwers, Song Shaoxiu (Taian Library) and Li Yindu (Public Education School); one triple jumper, Qu Baoqing (First Normal School); one long jumper and low hurdler, Tao Yongzhuang (First Normal School); one 10,000-meter runner, Ma Housheng (Zhengyi Middle School); one 800-meter runner, Zhang Shudong (First Middle School); one 400-meter runner, Ma Yu (Senior High School); one 200-meter runner, Han Yinshan (First Middle School); one high hurdler, Xu Lianpeng (Senior High School); one high jumper, Zhang Fangmei (First Normal School); one female 50-meter and 100-meter runner, Su Hui (First Girls' High School); and one female high jumper, Zhu Tianzhen (First Girls' Normal School). Today (the 24th) at 4 p.m., Wang Shulin, Chief of the Third Section of the Department of Education, and Zhang Zunsan, Director of the Public Sports Field, convened a meeting of all athletes in the Public Sports Field office to discuss departure matters. After the formal greetings, Wang Shulin and Zhang Zunsan gave encouraging speeches, saying, "You are shouldering a great responsibility in participating in the National Games in Hangzhou. We deeply hope that you will make extra efforts and win championships to bring glory to Shandong. In the future, all circles in Jinan will definitely hold a grand welcome ceremony to celebrate your success. Even if you fail, do not be discouraged, for failure is the mother of success. Return to Shandong and continue to work hard to win championships in future sports meets." The meeting adjourned at 5 p.m. It is reported that the athletes are scheduled to depart from Jinan by train to Shanghai to transfer to Hangzhou at 10:30 a.m. on the 25th. Each person will be given 40 yuan for travel expenses, and train tickets will be provided by the Department of Education. The Department of Education will also send Shang Xunsan, a physical education teacher from the Public School, to accompany and take care of everything. It is also reported that the names of those participating in the National Games from Shandong have been telegraphed to the National Games in Hangzhou by the Department of Education for registration.

News from the General Assembly Preparations 103

(1) Members of the Venue Committee

In addition to the list of committee members for the five divisions of the National Games Preparatory Office, namely, Affairs, Reception, Publicity, Awards, Arrangement, Transportation, and Tours, which has already been published in this newspaper, the list of members for the thirteen committees in the Venue Department is now recorded as follows: (1) Regulations Committee: Rong Qizhao, Ma Zhaohan, Qiu Jixiang, Zhang Xinfu, Shu Hong; (2) Venue Committee: Zhu Yaoting, Shu Hong, Yu Shifan, Zhu Qiangen; (3) Registration Committee: Zhang Xinfu, Wu Bangwei, Jiang Xiangqing, Zhang Zhongfan; (4) Order Committee: Hao Gengsheng, Zhang Zhongfan, Wu Bangwei, Wu Zhuozhi, Jiang Xiangqing; (5) Records Committee: Hao Boyang, Hao Gengsheng, Gao Xiwei, Xu Zhendong, Wu Bangwei, Tong Jiwu; (6) Referee Committee: Zhou Xiangxian, Huang Mingguo, Huang Yuandao, Hao Boyang, Ma Yuehan, Mo Yingyan, Xu Zhendong; (7) Track and Field and All-Around Committee: Ma Yuehan, Rong Qizhao, Lu Songen, Jin Zhaojun, Xie Wenqiu; (8) Swimming Committee: Ling Xitao, Zhu Peien, Tang Shuping, Xu Minhui, Yu Zhuohua; (9) Football Committee: Tong Jiwu, Wu Yanzhang, Le Xiurong, Yu Zhuohua, Wu Zhongjun; (10) Basketball Committee: Dong Shouyi, Zhang Guoxun, Shu Hong, Xu Zhendong, Zhang Huilan; (11) Tennis Committee: Wu Zhongguang, Ma Detai, Qiu Zhenglun, Lin Zuguang, Gao Zi; (12) Volleyball Committee: Xu Minhui, Wang Wenlin, Ou Bingguang, Gao Xiwei, Gu Gu Ruo; (13) Baseball Committee: Liu Dacheng, Lu Guanxiang, Zhang Guoxun, Du Tingxiu, Lin Zuguang.

(2) Distribution of Military Police Inside and Outside the Venue

Appropriately Deploy Military Police to Maintain the Venue: The General Assembly Preparatory Office, with the conference approaching, is eager to plan the security matters in advance. Therefore, it convened the first committee meeting yesterday. Those present were Yu Jimin, Zhou Bolang, Wu Wenbing, Shen Jihan, Cha Fuhua, and Gao Yun, with Wu Zhuozhi, Wu Bangwei, Shu Qian, Gu Luliang, Chai Xianrong, and Chen Miaoru in attendance. Yu Jimin chaired the meeting, and Chen Miaoru served as the recorder. The meeting proceeded as scheduled. The chairman proposed that the military police to maintain the General Assembly venue should be appropriately deployed from various military and police agencies. It was decided that 60 soldiers should be transferred from the Third Regiment of the Security Brigade, 60 soldiers from the Provincial Police Special Task Force, 50 soldiers from the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Cavalry Patrol, 50 patrolmen from the Second District Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and 10 soldiers from the Military Police Inspection Office. If the number is insufficient, temporary transfers will be made from the district offices of the Public Security Bureau, and 80 Boy Scouts will be deployed to maintain order inside the venue.

Distribution of Military Police Personnel at Various Locations: (1) Entrances and Exits: Each of the First, Second, Third, and Fourth entrances should be assigned one inspector, one squad leader, one patrol leader, and six military police. The Fifth entrance should be assigned one inspector, one squad leader, one patrol leader, and four military police. The Sixth entrance should be assigned one squad leader and three military police. Each exit should be assigned one military police officer. (2) Inside the Venue: The rostrum should be assigned two inspectors and thirty military police. The front of the western seating area of the track and field should be assigned ten military police. The eastern side of the track and field should be assigned two inspectors and twelve military police. The southern side of the track and field should be assigned one inspector and ten military police. The northern side of the athletes' seating area should be assigned five military police. The football field should be assigned three inspectors and forty military police. The basketball and volleyball court should be assigned two inspectors and twenty-four military police. The tennis court should be assigned two inspectors and twelve military police. The volleyball court should be assigned one inspector and six military police. The venue office should be assigned two inspectors and fourteen military police. (3) Outside the Venue: The road in front of the General Assembly should be assigned two inspectors and ten traffic police. The road in front of Dayingpan should be assigned one inspector and eight traffic police. The road west of the venue should be assigned five traffic police. The road east of the venue should be assigned three traffic police. Meidong High Bridge should be assigned two traffic police.

(3) Boy Scouts Maintain Order

In order to maintain order at the venue, the General Assembly sent a letter to the Municipal Government requesting that Boy Scouts be assigned to the venue to maintain order every day during the conference. The Municipal Government specially convened representatives from various schools yesterday to discuss the arrangements. Zong Wen Guo Huidi, Yan Zhong Yan Weiji, Anding Zhang Zhongwu, Huilan Lu Jingzeng, Municipal High School Gu Luliang, and Huixing Wang Zhen were present. Lu Buqing chaired the meeting. The meeting began as scheduled. A. The chairman reported the purpose of the meeting. B. Matters for discussion: (1) Allocation of personnel and dates. Resolution: Municipal High School: 160 people to serve for two days on April 1st and 2nd. Huilan: 240 people to serve for three days on April 7th, 8th, and 9th. Supervision High School: 160 people to serve for three days among April 3rd, 4th, 5th, and 6th. Anding: 80 people to serve for one day among April 3rd, 4th, 5th, and 6th. (2) Meal expenses issue. Resolution: Gu Luliang will attend the National Games to negotiate.

Guangdong Basketball Team Has Excellent Skills 107

Yesterday's Victory Over MacLaines… 50 to 34

After arriving in Shanghai, the Guangdong athletes have been practicing diligently, sparing no effort. Last night, the basketball team played a practice match with the American MacLaines team, starting at 9 p.m. at the China Basketball Stadium. As a result, Guangdong won with a score of 50 to 34. The referee was Xu Zhendong.

(1) MacLaines Used Their Second Team to Play

Regarding the situation of the two teams, MacLaines was slightly better in the first half, but the score was 19 points each. In the afternoon, the Guangdong team had a smooth run, and MacLaines had almost no power to resist. The Guangdong team is accustomed to playing four quarters, so last night's game was divided into four quarters. However, MacLaines used their second team to play, which slightly reduced the excitement of the game. Regarding the skills of the two teams, Huang Bingkun, the center of the Guangdong team, was good at both offense and defense, and his free throws were especially accurate. He and left forward Zhu Zucheng were equally outstanding. Li Lianying's defender frustrated the enemy's defense and was quite skilled. It is a pity that Guangdong frequently attacked with long shots, which does not seem like a good combat strategy. MacLaines' defender, Pankins, was quite skilled at long shots and hit them repeatedly. He was not easy to deal with.

(2) MacLaines Opened the Record

After the battle order was issued, both armies attacked and circled several times. MacLaines' left guard, Pankins, raised his hand for a long shot, which actually hit, thus opening the record. However, Zhu Zucheng, the left forward of the Guangdong team, also returned a long shot, leveling the situation. Pankins suddenly made repeated long shots again, hitting them every time, while Guangdong also tried long shots, but they seemed to have bad luck and did not succeed. MacLaines won the first quarter with a score of 11 to 5.

(3) Guangdong Team Showed Their Skills

Seeing that the situation was good, MacLaines changed five players to fight in the second quarter. The skills of offense and defense were not as good as the first five players. The Guangdong team quickly caught up, and their connection was good, and their power gradually showed. They moved forward step by step, reaching a score of 17 to 19. The first half ended at that time. Huang Bingkun scored another goal, making it a tie of 19 to 19.

(4) Guangdong Team Members Worked Hard to Connect

After a short break, MacLaines still used the first five players to participate in the battle. After this, the Guangdong team, in view of the failure of long shots, worked hard on cooperation and connection, and it really rose straight up. Huang Bingkun repeatedly broke through the barrier and went straight in. The third quarter ended, and Guangdong won with a score of 36 to 27.

(5) In the End, Guangdong Won

In the last quarter, the Guangdong team had a smooth run. MacLaines was under the strict surveillance of the Guangdong defenders and could not develop at all, falling into a state of panic. The three forwards of the Guangdong team used excellent connection and accurate shooting to win every section. In the end, the score was 50 to 34.

News

Opening on the Afternoon of April 15th, National Education Conference 110

The Standing Committee of the Preparatory Committee for the National Education Conference, held a meeting at 3:00 PM on the 25th at the Ministry of Education's conference room. All standing committee members (Vice Ministers, Directors, and Counselors) attended. They discussed matters related to the reception of attendees, such as how to accommodate the members (the Central Hotel is quite far from the Ministry of Railways venue, so arrangements were made with a car company for transportation times and methods, etc.), and other preparatory matters. The preparatory committee had initially drafted a schedule for the reception of members, which was about to be announced. However, after today's meeting, it was decided to postpone setting the schedule temporarily, to be announced ad hoc at the time of the opening, to allow for flexibility. As for the conference agenda, it has been largely set: The opening ceremony will be held at 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 15th (this day falls on a Tuesday, and key figures from the National Government will be unavailable due to the Executive Yuan meeting in the morning, so the opening ceremony was changed to the afternoon). The general meeting will be held on the morning of the 16th, and the review committee in the afternoon. From the 17th onwards, review committees will meet in the mornings and general meetings in the afternoons. On Sunday (the 20th), there will be a visit to the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum at Zaogu Temple in the morning, followed by lunch, and in the afternoon, a tour of the Ming Mausoleum and the Five Continents Park at Houhu Lake, with dinner at Central University. It is reported that after the National Education Conference, the directors of education from various provinces will stay for an extra day or two to hold an educational administrative conference to discuss communication between central and local educational administration. The Minister of Education has already asked the directors and counselors to prepare proposals for the administrative conference, it is said.

Nanjing Electric Dispatch on the 27th: The Ministry of Education has reassigned Zhu Jingnong as the Deputy Speaker of the National Education Conference, and Wu Yanin and Zhong Lingxiu as the secretaries of the venue. The conference venue will be the auditorium of the Ministry of Railways, and all rooms on the third floor of the Central Hotel have been reserved as dormitories for the members. The preparations for the conference are largely complete, and the preparatory committee is scheduled to meet on April 13th.

Jiangsu Education Department Convenes County Education Bureau Chiefs' Meeting (Part Two) 111

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The first meeting of county education bureau chiefs convened by the Jiangsu Education Department was held on the 24th in the Education Department's auditorium, as previously reported in this newspaper. On the mornings of the 25th and 26th, the various review committees met. It is said that there were many proposals, so the review has not yet concluded. During the afternoon meetings each day, the chairman designated four or five county education bureau chiefs to report on the special circumstances of education in their respective counties. The details of the meeting are recorded as follows:

(1) First Meeting

Held at 2 p.m. on the 24th in the Education Department. Chairman: Director Chen. Recorders: Zhang Jialin and Yang Changyun. (Reporting Items) 1. Section Chief Yang Naikang reported on the progress of the preparations and the number of attendees today. 2. Tian Shunlin, Director of the Jiangning County Education Bureau, and Zhang Shiming, Director of the Wuxi County Education Bureau, reported. (Discussion Items) 1. Proposals from various departments were submitted for review, and the chairman designated members of the group review committees (list provided separately). 2. The chairman proposed the establishment of an educational administration review committee. Resolution: Passed.

(2) Second Meeting

Held at 1 p.m. on the 25th. Chairman: Director Chen. Recorders: Zhang Jialin and Yang Changyun.

Reports were given by Han Wenqing, Director of the Zhenjiang County Education Bureau; Shi She, Director of the Shanghai County Education Bureau; Ni Shichang, Director of the Songjiang County Education Bureau; and Zhuang Yijian, Director of the Fengxian County Education Bureau.

(3) Third Meeting

Held at 1 p.m. on the 26th. Chairman: Director Chen. Reports on the local education situation were given by Zhang Zhihong, Director of the Chuansha County Education Bureau; Yang Shizeng, Director of the Jiading County Education Bureau; Min Yicheng, Director of the Wujin County Education Bureau; Rui Jiarui, Director of the Rugao County Education Bureau; Yao Gen, Inspector of Nantong County; and Gui Xinghai, Inspector of Changshu County. Section Chief Yang reported that a general meeting would be held at 9 a.m. tomorrow (the 27th) to discuss the proposals.

(4) Review Situation

Social Education Group: The Social Education Group review was held at 10 a.m. on the 25th. Chairman: Pan Yinge. Recorder: Liu Shuni. 1. Proposal on how to adapt county public education to social needs, improve people's lives, so as to realize local autonomy and complete the work of political tutelage (proposed by Kunshan, Zhenjiang, Nantong, and Fengxian counties). (Review Opinion) In accordance with the proposal and the original methods of each county, the Education Department will compile specific plans and implement them within a time limit. 2. Proposal on establishing public schools and first implementing a compulsory public education system (proposed by Songjiang). (Review Opinion) The original proposal intends to solve the problem of students being retained in public schools. It seems that appropriate improvements should first be made in the time, teaching materials, and teaching methods of the teaching. 3. Proposal on how to reorganize and expand social education institutions in various counties to improve the efficiency of social education (proposed by Zhenjiang, Kunshan, Nantong, and Fengxian counties). (Review Opinion) Please have the Education Department refer to the methods proposed by various counties, and separately order the counties to comply. 4. Proposal on how to effectively promote vocational supplementary education in various counties to develop people's production (proposed by Zhenjiang, Nantong, Kunshan, and Fengxian counties). (Review Opinion) Reference should be made to the methods proposed by Nantong, Zhenjiang, Kunshan, and Fengxian counties, and the Department should order each county to quickly establish a number of vocational supplementary schools based on local needs.

Party Doctrine Education Group: The Party Doctrine Education Group review was held on the 25th. Chairman: Feng Maiying. Recorder: Jiang Zhuoqun. (1) Discussion of solutions to the shortage of party doctrine teachers (Review Opinion) 1. If the number of qualified party doctrine teachers is insufficient, those who have a deep understanding of party doctrine and meet the qualifications of teachers may be temporarily appointed, not limited to party members. 2. Educational administrative organs should jointly with the county party headquarters, submit a request to organize party doctrine teacher training classes at their discretion. (2) Discussion of the allocation and addition of party doctrine courses (Review Opinion) 1. The county education bureau should convene the principals of primary and secondary schools and party doctrine teachers to make detailed allocations, which may be temporarily stipulated. 2. The aforementioned regulations shall be repealed immediately after the central government promulgates the standards for party doctrine courses. 3. Discussion of research on party doctrine curriculum teaching methods (Review Opinion) 1. Primary schools should focus on conversation design, such as using story teaching and narrating revolutionary events and historical facts of national humiliation, and participate in the basic explanation of the Three Principles of the People. 2. Senior primary schools should focus on design discussions, such as applying the aforementioned key points, and practice the initial steps of civil rights and pay attention to the essential points of nation-building strategies and nation-building outlines. (3) Junior high schools should focus on discussion and research, such as applying the aforementioned key points, and narrating Sun Yat-sen's theory, the history of national independence movements, and the study of unequal treaties and international situations. In addition, attention should be paid to the following three points: A. Party doctrine teaching should be linked with various subjects to form a whole.

Ministry of Education Investigates National Social Education 112

In order to investigate the status of social education in various provinces and cities across the country, the Ministry of Education has prepared a social education survey form and distributed it to various provinces and cities to be filled out. However, the previous form was relatively complex, and the procedures involved were numerous, making it difficult to fill out at once. Now, the Ministry of Education has reproduced two types of social education statistical survey forms for the 17th year for various provinces and cities, and has issued a notice to the education departments of various provinces and the education bureaus of special municipalities, requiring them to be submitted to the Ministry before the end of May.

Since the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department appointed Chen Jingchang as the principal of Songjiang Middle School, he has actively reformed school affairs, and the relationship between teachers and students is very harmonious. Since the beginning of this semester, students have initiated the organization of various academic research associations, such as the Music Research Association and the Drama Club.
